 alzimer ek ek maansik rog he, jiske kaaran marij kii yaaddaasht kamjor ho jaati he or uskaa asar dimag ke kaaryon par padataa he
 It is the most common type of dementia
 isse vyakti kii yaaddaasht, sochane kii kshamta, rosemara kii gatividhiyon par bura asar padataa he
 But a new study report suggests that consumption of green tea and carrots can reduce the risk of Alzheimer's
 yah study uniwarsity of southrn california ke shodhakartaaon dwaara kii gai he
 According to the Center for Disease Control and Prevention, Alzheimer's disease may catch more people in the coming times
 alzimer beemaari se jujh rahe logon ke vyaktitv, kaam karne, sochane, chizon ko yaad rakhane kii kshamta prabhavit hoti he
 In the study published in the Journal of Biological Chemistry, the team of researchers examined 2 compounds
 pehla ijisiji (EGCG) or doosraa ferulik acid (FA)
 EGCG is a type of antioxidant, which is found abundantly in green tea
 ye compound sharir main free radicals ko banane se roktaa he, jis kaaran sharir kii koshikaayen or maalicul damege hone se batch jate hai
 At the same time, some previous studies have reported that EGCG compound helps in securing new neurons, which does not weaken memory
 doosraa compound, ferulik acid (FA) he
 This compound is found in carrots, oats and tomatoes
 ferulik acid bhi ek tarah kaa antioxident he
 This antioxidant helps to overcome many skin related problems including sun burn, wrinkles
 yah study chuhon par kii gai he
 During the study, researchers divided Alzheimer's mice into 4 groups
 chaaron group main alzimer se peedit chuhon ke saath healdi chuuhe bhi shaamil kiye
 All these rats were given four different diets
 jo is prakaar hai- ek group ko ijisiji (EGCG) or ferulik acid (FA), duusare group ko sirf ijisiji (EGCG), tisare group ko sirf ferulik acid (FA) or chauthe group ko placebo diya gaya
 All mice were then examined
 nateezon main saamne aayaa jin chuhon ko ijisiji (EGCG) or ferulik acid (FA) diet di gai, unhone 3 maheenon ke andar healdi chuhon kii tarah hi parform kiya
 The lead author of the study, Dr
 terrence toun ne bataaya ki study aadhaar par kaha ja saktaa he ki ijisiji (EGCG) or ferulik acid (FA) dimag main amyloid beta protein ko pahunchane se rokte hai, jo yaaddaasht kamjor hone ke liye jimmedaar hote hai
 In addition, these antioxidants also play an important role in reducing brain tension

 twitter
 com / xfgyyvixfn Consumption of vitamin 'D' in high amounts is beneficial for the mental health of women and it reduces the risk of Alzheimer's (memory loss)
 america or france main kiye gaye do adhyayanon main yah baat saamne ai he
 The research, led by Yelena Slinin of the VA Medical Center in Minneapolis, found low levels of vitamin 'D' in women with Alzheimer's complaints
 is shodh main ek samudaay kii 6,257 bujurg mahilaon main vitamin 'di' ke str kii jaanch kii
 Researchers in France, led by Cedric Enviller, came to the conclusion after research on 498 women
 shodh ke anusaar jin mahilaon main alzimer tha ve vidamin di kii maatra prati hafte se 50
 Less than 3 micrograms were consumed in the diet while those suffering from dementia consumed less than 59 micrograms per week

 ' Makar Sankranti 2019: surya kaa kisi raashi vishesh par bhraman karnaa sankranti kehalaata he
 The Sun changes the zodiac sign in every month, so in total there are twelve Sankrantis in the year
 parantu do sankrantiyaan sarvaadhik mahatvapurn hoti hai-makar sankranti or kark sankranti
 Makar Sankranti occurs when the Sun enters Capricorn
 makar sankranti se agni tatva kii shuruyaat hoti he or kark sankranti se jal tatva kii
 At this time, the sun is Uttarayan, so the results of chanting and charity at this time are infinite times
 makar sankranti kaa jyotish se kya sambandh he?surya or shani kaa sambandh is parv se hone ke kaaran yah kaaphi mahatvapurn he
 It is believed that on this festival, Surya comes to meet his son Shani
 aam taur par shukr kaa udai bhi lagbhag isi samay hota he isliye yahaan se shubh kaaryon kii shuruyaat hoti he
 If the position of the Sun or Saturn in the horoscope is bad, then with special worship on this festival, you can correct it
 jahaan par parivaar main rog kalah tathaa ashaanti ho vahaan par rasoi ghar main grahon ke vishesh navann se puja karne se laabh hota he
 Makar Sankranti auspicious time (makar Sankranti Shubh Muhurat) Punya Kaal Muhurta - 07:14 to 12:36 (15 January 2019) Mahapunya Kaal Muhurta - 07:14 to 09:01 (15 January 2019) How to worship Makar Sankranti (makar Sankranti Pujan Vidhi) - Offer incense on Sun God
 - suryadev ke nimit til ke tel kaa deepak jalaaen
